name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Business travelers
info:18 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted April 5, 2024
msg:Kaiyue Shangcui is a young brand under Kaiyue. It mainly reflects and explores the geographical features of the hotel's location and is a window for hotel guests to understand the local culture. This hotel reflects the local mahjong culture of Ningbo, which is well reflected in the design and soft furnishing of the public areas. In particular, the mahjong wall of the three restaurants and the paintings in the lobby bar reflect this. The local map of Ningbo is also used as the decoration of the elevator hall and guest rooms through artistic techniques. The hotel is located in a commercial district, part of which is surrounded by an artificial lake. The hotel's facilities basically meet the five-star standard. The design of the public area is still a lot of effort. The reception desk is an island layout, which is very tonal. It has the flavor of Andaz and Indigo. The guest room is not large and the decoration is relatively simple. Because the opening is not large enough, the bathroom and shower room are separated into two layouts, leaving space for the entrance and dressing area. This design is still thoughtful. The facilities and supplies in the bathroom are average. The bedding is still very comfortable, and the electric curtains have good light blocking properties. In addition to the small sofa and small table by the window, there is also a floor-to-ceiling wooden box as a power socket, which better meets the office needs of business people. The bar is arranged near the window, which is quite convenient to use. The layout of this kind of guest room is still very novel. It's just that there is no room to put towels in the bathroom. After washing your hands, you have to go to the shower room to wipe your hands, which is inconvenient. The sound insulation effect of the guest room is not bad, and it is still very quiet all night. The commercial volume downstairs is still very large. Going downstairs and crossing a bridge is Kaiyuan Commercial Plaza. On the contrary, the business downstairs of the hotel is relatively quiet. The hotel's fitness center is on the 12th floor. The swimming pool is relatively small. It is operated by a third party and it feels that there are not many people. The gym is not big, and the equipment configuration is relatively general. It only meets general exercise. There is no barbell rack and no gym. I had lunch at Tongyuan 600 on the first floor of the hotel. The dishes are not large, but they are all relatively exquisite. The taste and service are impeccable, which better reflects the local salty and fresh characteristics of Ningbo. The hotel's breakfast is also here. There are not many varieties, but the noodles and wontons produced by the open stalls are still good. The vertical layout of the restaurant causes the dishes to be arranged more scattered, and the open counter is too short, so it is still crowded when there are many people. The hotel's underground garage is currently free parking. The hotel's service staff are relatively young, inexperienced but very enthusiastic. The hotel's room card is wooden and very distinctive. This hotel is located in Zhenhai District, Ningbo City, not the core area of ‚Äã‚ÄãNingbo City. It takes more than 20 minutes to drive to the center of Ningbo. Its location is not advantageous, but if you have the desire to explore this city, this hotel can also be an option.
